}
}

@keyframes preloader-floatingCanvas {
/*
Floating drift is applied on the parent container (.preloader__floating-canvas).
We want continuous motion, so drift accumulates across holds (no snap to 0 after each hold).

Drift is based on pure stage deltas (shuffling stage indices stays consistent):
D30 = (pos0 - pos3) * o
D01 = (pos1 - pos0) * o
D12 = (pos2 - pos1) * o
D23 = (pos3 - pos2) * o
*/

/* Loop boundary: begin 3→0 drift slightly before 0% */
0%,
100% {
transform: translate(
calc(
(var(--canvas-position-0-left) - var(--canvas-position-3-left)) *
var(--floating-offset) * 0.4
),
calc(
(var(--canvas-position-0-top) - var(--canvas-position-3-top)) *
var(--floating-offset) * 0.4
)
);
}

/* movement 0→1: keep at D30, then start drifting toward D30 + D01 slightly early */
20% {
transform: translate(
calc(
(var(--canvas-position-0-left) - var(--canvas-position-3-left)) *
var(--floating-offset)
),
calc(
(var(--canvas-position-0-top) - var(--canvas-position-3-top)) *
var(--floating-offset)
)
);
}

/* stage 1 hold: ramp to D30 + D01 */
36% {
transform: translate(
calc(
(
(var(--canvas-position-0-left) - var(--canvas-position-3-left)) +
(var(--canvas-position-1-left) - var(--canvas-position-0-left))
) * var(--floating-offset)
),
calc(
(
(var(--canvas-position-0-top) - var(--canvas-position-3-top)) +
(var(--canvas-position-1-top) - var(--canvas-position-0-top))
) * var(--floating-offset)
)
);
}

/* movement 1→2: keep at D30 + D01, then start drifting toward +D12 slightly early */
46% {
transform: translate(
calc(
(
(var(--canvas-position-0-left) - var(--canvas-position-3-left)) +
(var(--canvas-position-1-left) - var(--canvas-position-0-left)) +
(var(--canvas-position-2-left) - var(--canvas-position-1-left)) *
0.4
) * var(--floating-offset)
),
calc(
(
(var(--canvas-position-0-top) - var(--canvas-position-3-top)) +
(var(--canvas-position-1-top) - var(--canvas-position-0-top)) +
(var(--canvas-position-2-top) - var(--canvas-position-1-top)) *
0.4
) * var(--floating-offset)
)
);
}

/* movement 2→3: keep at D30 + D01 + D12, then start drifting toward +D23 slightly early */
68% {
transform: translate(
calc(
(
(var(--canvas-position-0-left) - var(--canvas-position-3-left)) +
(var(--canvas-position-1-left) - var(--canvas-position-0-left)) +
(var(--canvas-position-2-left) - var(--canvas-position-1-left))
) * var(--floating-offset)
),
calc(
(
(var(--canvas-position-0-top) - var(--canvas-position-3-top)) +
(var(--canvas-position-1-top) - var(--canvas-position-0-top)) +
(var(--canvas-position-2-top) - var(--canvas-position-1-top))
) * var(--floating-offset)
)
);
}
/* stage 3 hold: ramp to D30 + D01 + D12 + D23 (loop closure, equals 0) */
88% {
transform: translate(
calc(
(
(var(--canvas-position-0-left) - var(--canvas-position-3-left)) +
(var(--canvas-position-1-left) - var(--canvas-position-0-left)) +
(var(--canvas-position-2-left) - var(--canvas-position-1-left)) +
(var(--canvas-position-3-left) - var(--canvas-position-2-left))
) * var(--floating-offset)
),
calc(
(
(var(--canvas-position-0-top) - var(--canvas-position-3-top)) +
(var(--canvas-position-1-top) - var(--canvas-position-0-top)) +
(var(--canvas-position-2-top) - var(--canvas-position-1-top)) +
(var(--canvas-position-3-top) - var(--canvas-position-2-top))
) * var(--floating-offset)
)
);
}
}

(() => {
window.addEventListener('CLASSIC_EDITOR_LOADED', onEditorLoaded, {
once: true,
});

function onEditorLoaded() {
const progressbar = document.querySelector('.preloader__progress');
if (!progressbar) return;

const clipper = progressbar.querySelector('.preloader__progress-clipper');
const visual = progressbar.querySelector('.preloader__progress-visual');

if (!clipper || !visual) return;

// Step 1: Get current animated transform values
const clipperTransform = window.getComputedStyle(clipper).transform;
const visualTransform = window.getComputedStyle(visual).transform;

// Step 2: Stop animations and freeze at current position
clipper.style.animation = 'none';
visual.style.animation = 'none';
clipper.style.transform = clipperTransform;
visual.style.transform = visualTransform;

// Step 3: Force reflow to apply the frozen state
void clipper.offsetHeight;

// Step 4: Add transition on next frame and set final values
requestAnimationFrame(() => {
progressbar.classList.add('preloader__progress_complete');
});
}
})();
